## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: population ecology / mathematical biology (population dynamics)
**Analysis**: The variables describe a single-species population P(t) and its instantaneous growth rate dP_dt, which is the standard setup for deterministic population dynamics ODEs. Most classical relationships express dP_dt as per-capita growth times P, often modified by density dependence, Allee effects, harvesting, and environmental (time) forcing.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Exponential (Malthusian) growth: dP_dt = c0 * P (constant per-capita growth/decline, low-density regime)
- Linear + density term: dP_dt = (c0 + c1 * t) * P (time-trending growth rate due to changing environment/resources)
- Periodic forcing of growth rate: dP_dt = (c0 + c1 * sin(c2 * t)) * P (seasonal reproduction/mortality)
- Ricker-type density dependence (exponential crowding): dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - exp(c1 * P)) (rapid suppression at high density)
- Verhulst logistic ODE form: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) (crowding via quadratic self-limitation; carrying capacity implicit)
- Generalized (theta) logistic: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P) ** c2) (flexible density-dependence curvature)
- Gompertz growth ODE: dP_dt = c0 * P * log(c1 / P) (decelerating growth; multiplicative noise/size-scaling contexts)
- Richards growth (shape-parameter generalization): dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P) ** c2) ** c3 (adjustable sigmoidal shape beyond theta-logistic)
- Allee effect (strong Allee, cubic): dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) * (c2 * P - 1) (reduced growth at low density; extinction threshold)
- Allee effect (weak Allee, quadratic modifier): dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) * (1 + c2 * P) (facilitation at low/moderate density without strict threshold)
- Constant-yield harvesting: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) - c2 (quota harvest; can drive collapse if too large)
- Proportional harvesting/mortality: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) - c2 * P (effort-based harvest or added mortality)
- Saturating harvest (Holling type II on removal): dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) - c2 * P / (P + c3) (handling-time-limited harvesting/predation)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Per-capita growth modeling: writing dP_dt = P * g(P,t) encodes that zero population implies zero births and allows interpreting g as net per-capita rate.
- Density dependence strength: appearance of a negative P^2 term (e.g., -c*P^2 inside dP_dt) indicates crowding/competition limiting growth at high P.
- Carrying-capacity-like behavior: factors of the form (1 - c*P) or (1 - (c*P)^theta) imply an equilibrium near P ≈ 1/c (or (1/c) for theta=1).
- Gompertz mechanism: a log(c/P) factor means per-capita growth decreases roughly linearly with log(P), common when proportional growth slows with size/scale.
- Allee effects: additional low-density suppressive factors (e.g., (c*P - 1)) create a critical threshold where dP_dt changes sign at small P.
- Harvest signatures: subtracting c (constant yield) or c*P (proportional removal) shifts equilibria downward and can introduce bistability/collapse.
- Seasonality/time forcing: sin(c*t) or cos(c*t) inside the growth coefficient indicates periodic environmental modulation of births/deaths.
- Changing environment: polynomial-in-t coefficients (c0 + c1*t + ...) suggest gradual trends in habitat quality/resources affecting growth rate over time.

============================================================
GT Equivalence Verification (BPG13)
============================================================
GT: c0*(-c1 + P/c2)*(c3 - P/c4)*P + c5*P + c6*P/(c7 + exp(-c8*(-c9 + P)))
Candidate formulas: 50

Let \(F_{\text{GT}}(t,P)\) be the fixed ground-truth function:
\[
F_{\text{GT}}(t,P)=0.2010739\Big(-1+\frac{P}{5.6365765}\Big)\Big(1-\frac{P}{10.2325613}\Big)P\;+\;0.2010739\,P\;+\;0.2010739\,\frac{P}{1+\exp\!\big(-5.6365765(P-0.6341847)\big)}.
\]
Key structural facts:

- **No \(t\)-dependence at all**. So any candidate containing \(\sin(\cdot t)\), \(\cos(\cdot t)\), \(\exp(c t)\), \(\log(c t+1)\), etc. must have those terms forced to zero (by setting their coefficients to 0) to match for all \(t\).
- As a function of \(P\), GT is **(cubic polynomial in \(P\)) + (logistic-type term)**:
  \[
  \text{poly}_3(P) \;+\; K\cdot \frac{P}{1+\exp(-a(P-b))},
  \]
  with \(K,a\neq 0\). This logistic term is **not** representable as a polynomial, rational function, trig, or log of algebraic expressions in \(P\) unless the candidate explicitly contains a matching logistic/exponential-in-\(P\) denominator structure (none do).

So a candidate can only match if it can reproduce **both**:
1) the cubic polynomial part, and  
2) the non-polynomial logistic term \(\propto \frac{P}{1+\exp(-a(P-b))}\).

GT Equivalence Verification (BPG13)
============================================================
GT: c0*(-c1 + P/c2)*(c3 - P/c4)*P + c5*P + c6*P/(c7 + exp(-c8*(-c9 + P)))
Candidates evaluated: 50
Matched candidate IDs: []
Matched candidates: []

I need to analyze the Ground Truth (GT) expression and compare it with each candidate.

## GT Analysis

The GT is:
```
0.201*(-1 + P/5.637)*(1 - P/10.233)*P + 0.201*P + 0.201*P/(1 + exp(-5.637*(-0.634 + P)))
```

Let me expand the first term:
- (-1 + P/5.637)(1 - P/10.233) = -1 + P/10.233 + P/5.637 - P²/(5.637×10.233)
- Multiplied by P: -P + P²/10.233 + P²/5.637 - P³/(5.637×10.233)

So GT = 0.201*[-P + P²/10.233 + P²/5.637 - P³/57.68] + 0.201*P + 0.201*P/(1 + exp(-5.637*(P - 0.634)))

The 0.201*(-P) + 0.201*P cancels out!

GT = 0.201*[P²/10.233 + P²/5.637 - P³/57.68] + 0.201*P/(1 + exp(-5.637*(P - 0.634)))

GT = 0.201*P²*(1/10.233 + 1/5.637) - 0.201*P³/57.68 + 0.201*P/(1 + exp(-5.637*(P - 0.634)))

So GT has the form:
**c0*P³ + c1*P² + sigmoid_term(P)**

The sigmoid term is: 0.201*P/(1 + exp(-5.637*(P-0.634)))

This is a function of P only (no t dependence).

Key structural features:
1. **No dependence on t** - GT is purely a function of P
2. Contains P³, P², and a sigmoid-like term: P/(1 + exp(...))

Now let me check each candidate:

**Candidates with t-dependence that cannot be zeroed out:**
- Candidates 1, 4, 5, 8, 12, 13, 14, 25, 30, 32, 33, 35, 39, 43, 46, 47, 48: contain sin(t), cos(t), exp(t), or log(t) terms. If these can be zeroed by setting coefficients to 0, the remaining terms must match GT.

For candidates where t-terms can be zeroed, I need to check if the remaining P-terms can match GT.

**GT structure after simplification:** P³*a + P²*b + P/(1 + exp(α*(P - β)))

The sigmoid term P/(1+exp(-5.637*(P-0.634))) is crucial. Let me check which candidates have a sigmoid-like term or equivalent.

**Candidates 6, 7, 15, 16, 17, 18, 19:** These have terms like P*c*(P³*c + 1)**c which is NOT a sigmoid.

**Candidates 42, 49:** Have P*c/(P+c) which is a rational function, plus log terms - not sigmoid.

**Candidate 25:** P³c0 + P²c1 + Pc2 + P^c3*c4*sin(c5*t+c6) + c7*log(c8*exp(P*c9)+1). Setting c4=0 to kill sin term: P³c0 + P²c1 + Pc2 + c7*log(c8*exp(Pc9)+1). The log(c8*exp(Pc9)+1) is a softplus-like function, NOT P/(1+exp(...)). **No match.**

**Candidate 46:** c4*log(c5*exp(Pc6 + c7*sin(...))+1). Setting c7=0: c4*log(c5*exp(Pc6)+1) = softplus, not sigmoid. **No match.**

After careful analysis, none of the candidates contain a term of the form P/(1+exp(f(P))) which is the sigmoid multiplied by P. The closest structures involve log(exp+1) (softplus), rational functions P/(P+c), or (P³c+1)^c (power functions), none of which are equivalent to the sigmoid term.

Let me verify: No candidate has the structural form P/(1 + exp(g(P))).

Candidate 1-50 verdict analysis: None contain the required sigmoid term P/(1+exp(αP+β)).

Candidate 1 through 50 verdict: [NO MATCH] for all.
